Q:How many uniquegoalkeapers took part in all seasons?
SQL: SELECT COUNT(T1.Player) FROM (SELECT Player FROM nhl WHERE Pos = 'G' GROUP BY Player HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT Season) = (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT Season) FROM nhl)) AS T1
Result: [{'COUNT(T1.Player)': 0}]

Q:How many goalkeapers took part in all seasons?
SQL: SELECT COUNT(T1.Player) FROM (SELECT Player FROM nhl WHERE Pos = 'G' GROUP BY Player HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT Season) = (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT Season) FROM nhl)) AS T1
Result: [{'COUNT(T1.Player)': 0}]

Q:How many uniquegoalkeapers took part in season 2008-2009?
SQL: SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT Player) FROM nhl_2004_2018_player_data WHERE Pos = 'G' AND Season = 2009
Result: [{'COUNT(DISTINCT Player)': 0}]
